Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 44, the initial release (though not the final mission release) of the Apollo 10 Command Module (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software. Subsequent releases were Comanche 45 and Comanche 45/2 (the flown release on Apollo 10). The reconstruction is believed to be exactly accurate, but in the absence of an actual Apollo-era listing of Comanche 44, some explanation of the reconstruction process is needed to insure confidence in that accuracy.

The starting point was the source code of Comanche 51 (separately previously reconstructed from an Apollo-era listing of Comanche 55, flown on Apollo 11). Comanche 51 source code was then modified by undoing changes known to have been made between revisions 44 and 51. The now-reconstructed Comanche 44 source code was verified by assembling it and checking that the assembled code had the expected known-correct memory-bank checksums. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Comanche 55 printout, although the source code would likely have different page numbers in a contemporary Comanche 44 listing.

Annotations that were not present in the contemporary source code have been added to the reconstructed code to justify each change relative to Comanche 51. Here's a guide to the Apollo documentation referenced in those annotations:
  • MIT/IL engineering drawing 2021153D, sheet 3. Listing of the memory-bank checksums for Comanche 44.
  • Comanche 55 (Apollo 11 CM final release) assembly listing.
  • Reconstructed Comanche 51 (Apollo 11 CM initial release) assembly listing.
  • Colossus 249 (Apollo 9 CM final release) assembly listing.
  • Guidance System Operations Plan for Colossus 3, Section 5, p. xiii. Table listing some Program Request Changes (PCRs) incorporated between Comanche 45/2 and Comanche 55.
  • Guidance System Operations Plan for Colossus 2E, Section 3, pp. ix-x. Tables listing some Program Change Requests (PCRs) incorporated between Comanche 44 and Comanche 55.
  • Programmed Guidance Equations for Colossus 2, Based on Comanche 55. Provides a pseudocode representation of portions of Comanche 55, showing change bars. The software revisions from which and to which the changes occurred are indicated by the markings next to the document page number:
    • "Rev. 0" pages: change bars are from Colossus 249 to Comanche 45
    • "Rev. 1" pages: change bars are from Comanche 45 to Comanche 45/2
    • "Rev. 2" pages: change bars are from Comanche 45/2 to Comanche 55
In most cases, only the titles (rather than the full texts) of PCRs are known. In addition to the explanatory annotations, there is also a step-by-step commentary about the reconstruction process.

Comments expected to have been present in the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC Project's GitHub repository. 

001623,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001624,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001625,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Comanche revision 044.
001626,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the
001627,000006:                                                                                                  ##              original release of the flight software for the Command
001628,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10.
001629,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a copy of Comanche 055. It
001630,000009:                                                                                                  ##              has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
001631,000010:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Comanche 44 in NASA drawing
001632,000011:                                                                                                  ##              2021153D, which gives relatively high confidence that the
001633,000012:                                                                                                  ##              reconstruction is correct.
001634,000013:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001635,000014:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001636,000015:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
001637,000016:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2020-12-03 MAS  Created from Comanche 51.

001639,000018:                                                                                                  ##                              STARSAV3.

001645,000024:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001646,000025: 
001647,000026:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001648,000027:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001649,000028:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001650,000029: 
001651,000030:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  START
001652,000031:                                                                                                  #                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001653,000032:                                                                                                  #                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001654,000033: 
001655,000034:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001656,000035:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001657,000036:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.                )
001658,000037: 
001659,000038:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001660,000039:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001661,000040: 
001662,000041:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  Y
001663,000042: 
001664,000043:                                                                                                  #        =       MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001665,000044:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001666,000045: 
001667,000046:                                                                                                  #                        X       =       Y
001668,000047: 
001669,000048:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001670,000049:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001671,000050: 
001672,000051:                                                                                                  #                M       REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001673,000052:                                                                                                  #                        B       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001674,000053:                                                                                                  #                                INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001675,000054:                                                                                                  #                        I       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001676,000055:                                                                                                  #                                INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001677,000056:                                                                                                  #                                INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001678,000057: 
001679,000058:                                                                                                  #                SIZE    IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001680,000059: 
001681,000060:                                                                                                  #                N       INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001682,000061:                                                                                                  #                        PL      MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001683,000062:                                                                                                  #                        DSP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001684,000063:                                                                                                  #                        PRM     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001685,000064:                                                                                                  #                                IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001686,000065:                                                                                                  #                                PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001687,000066:                                                                                                  #                        TMP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001688,000067:                                                                                                  #                                IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001689,000068:                                                                                                  #                                IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001690,000069:                                                                                                  #                                PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001691,000070:                                                                                                  #                                CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 38 

001693,000072:                                                                                                  #                                IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001694,000073:                                                                                                  #                                IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001695,000074:                                                                                                  #                        IN      MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001696,000075:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001697,000076:                                                                                                  #                        OUT     MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001698,000077:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001699,000078:

001704,000083: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001705,000084: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001706,000085: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001707,000086: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001708,000087: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001709,000088: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001710,000089: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001711,000090:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001712,000091: 
001713,000092: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001714,000093: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001715,000094: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001716,000095: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.

001718,000097: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001719,000098: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.

Reconstruction: Relative to Comanche 51, the variables EK2VAL and EK3VAL have been removed at this point. This is justified by Programmed Guidance Equations for Colossus 2, p. 91, which indicates that those variables first appeared between Comanche 45/2 and Comanche 55. That reference also indicates a change in the variable FANG; this is due not to a change in the line of code, but rather because removing EK2VAL and EK3VAL had changed the address at which the instruction appears in memory. (A change of E3J22R2M and E32C31RM is also indicated, but those variables had not yet been introduced in Comanche 51, and therefore did not need to be removed in the reconstruction of Comanche 44.)
